def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:AccountShortInquiryReq">
<accountNum>114462537</accountNum>
<options>8</options>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

> assert(i != -1)

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:AccountShortInquiryReq">
<accountNum>114462537</accountNum>
<options>8</options>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

E assert -1 != -1
